[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m:mkdir -p $[0m[1;39m{[0m[39mBUILD_DIR[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m:pushd $[0m[1;39m{[0m[39mBUILD_DIR[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m:meson setup .. -[0m[33mDtestdata_tests[0m[39m=[0m[35mtrue[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m8[0m[39m:ninja[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m9[0m[39m:meson test -v[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Overview and Root Cause  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   The permission error [0m[1;39m([0m[39mexit code [0m[1;36m126[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m arises because the fuzzer executables [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`dav1d_fuzzer` and `dav1d_fuzzer_mt`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are built by Meson but never marked as [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minstallable artifacts. OSS-Fuzzâ€™s build/packaging pipeline [0m[1;39m([0m[39mand the Docker runner[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrelies on Mesonâ€™s install rules [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi.e. `ninja install` or `meson install`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to place [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbinaries into the `$OUT` directory with the correct executable bits. Since the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzzer targets lack `install: true`, they are omitted from the install step [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcopied without +x[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, leading to â€œPermission deniedâ€ when the harness tries to [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexecute `[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer_mt[0m[39m`.[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Preserve Existing Logic  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We do not alter any harness code, fuzzing logic, or test scripts.  [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The existing Meson build for the main `dav1d` CLI tool already uses `install: [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtrue`; we mirror that pattern for fuzzers.  [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Build-by-default remains enabled so fuzzers continue to compile in every [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuild.[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch Steps  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   A. Open `tests/libfuzzer/meson.build` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m61[0m[39mâ€“[0m[1;36m70[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and locate both fuzzer [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexecutable definitions:  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - `dav1d_fuzzer`  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - `dav1d_fuzzer_mt`  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   B. For each `[0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` call, add the install parameters:  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      â€¢ install: true  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      â€¢ install_dir: [0m[1;35mget_option[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'bindir'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m   [0m[1;39m([0m[39mso they end up in the standard `bin/` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpath under the install prefix[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   C. The updated snippet for `dav1d_fuzzer_mt` will resemble:[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      dav1d_fuzzer_mt = [0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[32m'dav1d_fuzzer_mt'[0m[39m,[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        dav1d_fuzzer_sources,[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        include_directories: dav1d_inc_dirs,[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        c_args: [0m[1;39m[[0m[32m'-DDAV1D_MT_FUZZING'[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        link_args: fuzzer_ldflags,[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        link_with: libdav1d,[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        install: true,[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        install_dir: [0m[1;35mget_option[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'bindir'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m,[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        build_by_default: true,[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        dependencies: [0m[1;39m[[0m[39mthread_dependency[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        kwargs: fuzzer_link_lang[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   D. Apply the same `install` block to `dav1d_fuzzer`.[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Validation in OSS-Fuzz Build  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The standard OSS-Fuzz Meson-based pipeline will invoke `meson install` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ninja install`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m after the build step, copying all `install: true` targets into [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`$OUT/bin` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmounted as `[0m[35m/[0m[95mout[0m[39m` in the Docker runner[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Since Meson preserves the executable bit on installed executables, the fuzzers[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwill now be runnable by the harness.  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No changes are required to the harness or Docker configuration.[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Rationale and Side-Effect Mitigation  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This minimally invasive change leverages Mesonâ€™s built-in installation [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmechanism, aligning the fuzzer targets with the projectâ€™s existing install [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconventions.  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - It avoids any direct chmod hacks or post-build scripts, ensuring [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmaintainability.  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No broader utility functions or other targets are modified, reducing risk.  [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If any downstream process does not automatically invoke `ninja install`, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mensure the OSS-Fuzz build definition includes the install step [0m[1;39m([0m[39mstandard practice[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Similar Precedent  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The main CLI tool `dav1d` in `tools/meson.buil[0m[1;92md:109[0m[39mâ€“[0m[1;36m123[0m[39m` already uses [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`install: true`. We follow the same pattern for fuzzers to guarantee consistent [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdeployment.  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Summary of the root cause  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   The â€œPermission deniedâ€ error arises because the Meson build definitions for [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mboth fuzzers [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`dav1d_fuzzer` and `dav1d_fuzzer_mt`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m do not specify `install: true`.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mIn OSS-Fuzzâ€™s build process, after compilation, a `ninja install` stage [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwith [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`--[0m[33mprefix[0m[39m=$OUT`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m stages all â€œinstalledâ€ targets into `$OUT`. Targets without [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`install: true` are never installed and thus, when OSS-Fuzzâ€™s wrapper copies or [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msymlinks built binaries into `[0m[35m/[0m[95mout[0m[39m`, they may lack executable bits or simply not be[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpicked up correctly, resulting in a non-executable file under `[0m[35m/[0m[95mout[0m[39m`.[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Patch outline  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   In `tests/libfuzzer/meson.build`, for each `[0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` block defining a [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzzer, add the Meson keyword argument `install: true`. This aligns these targets [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwith the existing DAV1D CLI target in `tools/meson.build`, which already uses [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`install: true` and thereby ensures correct installation mode [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0755[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and placement [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munder the install prefix. Specifically:[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - After `build_by_default: true`, add `install: true` to both the `dav1d_fuzzer`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand `dav1d_fuzzer_mt` definitions.[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No changes are made to harness code, external libraries, or test code; [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexisting build logic and fuzzer flags remain untouched.[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Detailed steps  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Open `tests/libfuzzer/meson.build`.  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Locate the `dav1d_fuzzer` executable block:[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```meson[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      dav1d_fuzzer = [0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'dav1d_fuzzer'[0m[39m,[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          dav1d_fuzzer_sources,[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          include_directories: dav1d_inc_dirs,[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          link_args: fuzzer_ldflags,[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          link_with : libdav1d,[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          build_by_default: true,[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          dependencies : [0m[1;39m[[0m[39mthread_dependency[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          kwargs: fuzzer_link_lang[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      Insert `install: true,` immediately after `build_by_default: true,` so it [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbecomes:[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```meson[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      dav1d_fuzzer = [0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'dav1d_fuzzer'[0m[39m,[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          dav1d_fuzzer_sources,[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          include_directories: dav1d_inc_dirs,[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          link_args: fuzzer_ldflags,[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          link_with : libdav1d,[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          build_by_default: true,[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          install: true,[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          dependencies : [0m[1;39m[[0m[39mthread_dependency[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          kwargs: fuzzer_link_lang[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Do the same for `dav1d_fuzzer_mt`:[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```meson[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      dav1d_fuzzer_mt = [0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'dav1d_fuzzer_mt'[0m[39m,[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          dav1d_fuzzer_sources,[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          include_directories: dav1d_inc_dirs,[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          c_args: [0m[1;39m[[0m[32m'-DDAV1D_MT_FUZZING'[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          link_args: fuzzer_ldflags,[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          link_with : libdav1d,[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          build_by_default: true,[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          install: true,[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          dependencies : [0m[1;39m[[0m[39mthread_dependency[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          kwargs: fuzzer_link_lang[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. Rebuild and reinstall:[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Rerun Meson and Ninja:[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        meson setup builddir --[0m[33mprefix[0m[39m=$OUT -[0m[33mDfuzzing_engine[0m[39m=[0m[35moss[0m[39m-fuzz[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ninja -C builddir[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ninja -C builddir install[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Verify that `[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer_mt[0m[39m` and `[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer[0m[39m` are present with[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`rwxr-xr-x` permissions.[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Mirrors the existing pattern for the main `dav1d` CLI tool in [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`tools/meson.build` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhich already has `install: true`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, ensuring that fuzzer [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbinaries are treated identically.  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Guarantees the binaries are placed into the installation prefix [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`$OUT`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m with [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe executable bit set, eliminating the â€œPermission deniedâ€ failure.  [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Does not alter any fuzzing harness, test code, or external dependencies. All [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moriginal build flags, sanitizers, and threading logic remain intact.[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential side effects and mitigation  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No runtime behavior of the fuzzer itself changes. Only installation metadata [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mis affected.  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Build time increases negligibly due to the `install` step, but this is [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstandard for OSS-Fuzz.  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Downstream tests and CI jobs that rely on the fuzzer binaries being executable[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwill now pass.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause & Key Insight  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `dav1d_fuzzer` and `dav1d_fuzzer_mt` targets in [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`tests/libfuzzer/meson.build` lack the `install: true` parameter.  [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Without `install: true`, Meson does not install these executables into the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minstall prefix during `ninja install`, causing OSS-Fuzzâ€™s staging logic to pick up [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39ma non-executable placeholder [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor a file with wrong permissions[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m under `[0m[35m/[0m[95mout[0m[39m`.  [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - As a result, `[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer_mt[0m[39m` exists but is not marked executable, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mleading to the â€œPermission deniedâ€ [0m[1;39m([0m[39mexit [0m[1;36m126[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m error when the fuzzer wrapper tries [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto run it.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Strategy to Fix  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   A. Amend Meson build definitions for both fuzzer targets so that they are [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mproperly installed with execute permissions:  [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Edit `tests/libfuzzer/meson.build` around lines [0m[1;36m51[0m[39mâ€“[0m[1;36m59[0m[39m and [0m[1;36m61[0m[39mâ€“[0m[1;36m70[0m[39m.  [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - For each `[0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` invocation [0m[1;39m([0m[39msingle-threaded and multi-threaded [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzzer[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, add the named argument `install: true`.  [0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - This ensures that when `ninja install --[0m[33mprefix[0m[39m=$OUT` runs, Meson will copy [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe built binaries into the install prefix [0m[1;39m([0m[39mand OSS-Fuzzâ€™s infrastructure will [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstage them under `[0m[35m/[0m[95mout[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m with the correct `+x` bit.  [0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   B. Preserve Existing Logic  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - All other parameters [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`build_by_default`, `link_args`, `dependencies`, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39metc.[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remain untouched to avoid affecting linking flags or build order.  [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - No changes to harness code, wrapper scripts, or C/C++ sourceâ€”only the Meson[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuild manifest is updated.  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Tests and external tools continue to locate `[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer[0m[1;39m[[0m[39m_mt[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` as [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbefore; now the files will be executable.  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   C. Implementation Steps  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Open `tests/libfuzzer/meson.build`.  [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Locate the block defining `dav1d_fuzzer` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines ~[0m[1;36m51[0m[39mâ€“[0m[1;36m59[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:  [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         ```meson[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         dav1d_fuzzer = [0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'dav1d_fuzzer'[0m[39m,[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             dav1d_fuzzer_sources,[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             include_directories: dav1d_inc_dirs,[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             link_args: fuzzer_ldflags,[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             link_with: libdav1d,[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             build_by_default: true,[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             dependencies: [0m[1;39m[[0m[39mthread_dependency[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             kwargs: fuzzer_link_lang,[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             install: true   # <â€” Add this line[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         ```  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Locate the block defining `dav1d_fuzzer_mt` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines ~[0m[1;36m61[0m[39mâ€“[0m[1;36m70[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:  [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         ```meson[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         dav1d_fuzzer_mt = [0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'dav1d_fuzzer_mt'[0m[39m,[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             dav1d_fuzzer_sources,[0m                                                  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             kwargs: fuzzer_link_lang,[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             install: true   # <â€” Add this line[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         ```  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Commit these changes and re-run the OSS-Fuzz build [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhich performs `ninja [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minstall --[0m[33mprefix[0m[39m=$OUT`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. Verify in CI logs that `[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer_mt[0m[39m` and `[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer[0m[39m` are [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpresent with `rwxr-xr-x` permissions and that the fuzzer binaries execute without [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpermission errors.  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Justification & Risk Mitigation  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Optimality**: This patch directly addresses the missing install directive, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrestoring the execute bit at the point of installation.  [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Minimal Impact**: Only the Meson manifest is modified; no functional code, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mharness scripts, or external dependencies are touched.  [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Preserves Functionality**: Existing flags, build dependencies, and linking [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msemantics remain unchanged.  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Side Effects**: Downstream logic that expects these targets to be installed [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwill now find them in the install prefix; no adverse side effects are expected.  [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Precedent**: The main `dav1d` CLI tool in `meson.build` uses `install: [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtrue`, confirming this pattern for deliverable executables.[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. No Further Patches Required  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The duplicate flags in the fuzzer invocation [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., two `-runs`, two [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`-timeout`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m do not impede execution and should be left for a separate hygiene [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcleanup if desired.  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Permission issues will be resolved once the install bit is properly set.  [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No modifications to harness, Dockerfile, or run scripts are needed.  [0m          [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Preserve all other arguments and dependencies:[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Do not change or remove `c_args`, `link_args`, `link_with`, `dependencies`, or[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`kwargs`.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Keep `build_by_default: true` unchanged to ensure the fuzzer targets are still[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuilt by default.[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Rebuild under OSS-Fuzz:[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Verify that the build step calls `meson install --[0m[33mdestdir[0m[39m=$OUT` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mas per [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstandard OSS-Fuzz Meson integration[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Confirm that `[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer[0m[39m` and `[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer_mt[0m[39m` exist and have [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`rwx` permissions for the running user.[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Rerun the fuzzer harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`run_fuzzer dav1d_fuzzer_mt [0m[33m...[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and ensure the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mâ€œPermission deniedâ€ error no longer occurs.[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJustification:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Meson's `install:` flag is the proper mechanism to mark built targets for [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minstallation into `$OUT`. Without these directives, OSS-Fuzzâ€™s installation phase [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msilently omits them, and any files manually copied or mounted lack executable bits.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This strategy does not alter any test or harness code, nor does it modify [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexternal dependencies. It only affects the projectâ€™s own build configuration.[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Adding `install: true, install_dir: [0m[32m'.'[0m[39m` is minimally invasive and follows the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mestablished pattern in other Meson-based OSS-Fuzz integrations, restoring the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexpected behavior without side effects.[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Existing fuzzer logic, threading flags [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., `-DDAV1D_MT_FUZZING`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, and [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcompiler/linker options remain unmodified, so runtime behavior of the fuzzers is [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munchanged aside from proper invocation permissions.[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m70[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtests/libfuzzer/meson.buil[0m[1;92md:61[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m70[0m                                                   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m61:da[0m[39mv1d_fuzzer_mt = [0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'dav1d_fuzzer_mt'[0m[39m,[0m                                  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m64[0m[39m:    c_args: [0m[1;39m[[0m[32m'-DDAV1D_MT_FUZZING'[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m65[0m[39m:    link_args: fuzzer_ldflags,[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m66[0m[39m:    link_with : libdav1d,[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m67[0m[39m:    build_by_default: true,[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m68[0m[39m:    dependencies : [0m[1;39m[[0m[39mthread_dependency[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m69[0m[39m:    kwargs: fuzzer_link_lang[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m70[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause & Symptoms  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The â€œPermission deniedâ€ [0m[1;39m([0m[39mexit code [0m[1;36m126[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m occurs because OSS-Fuzzâ€™s runner [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmounts the `$OUT` directory containing the fuzzer binaries, but those binaries [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39meither [0m[1;39m([0m[39ma[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are not present in `$OUT`, or [0m[1;39m([0m[39mb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m lack the executable bit when the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontainer invokes `[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer_mt[0m[39m`.  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The existing `.aixcc/test.sh` script only configures and builds the project [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munder `build/` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvia Meson/Ninja[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and runs tests, but never installs or copies the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresulting fuzzers into `$OUT`, nor does it ensure they are executable.  [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Critical Logic to Preserve  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We must preserve the Meson/Ninja build steps and the existing test invocation [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`meson test -v`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We must not modify harness code or fuzzing logic; only the OSS-Fuzz test [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdriver [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`.aixcc/test.sh`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is in scope.  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We must continue to build both `dav1d_fuzzer` and `dav1d_fuzzer_mt` under [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`build/tests/libfuzzer/`.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Proposed Patch Location  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - File: `.aixcc/test.sh` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe OSS-Fuzz test driver script[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Immediately after the existing build/test steps, append logic to [0m[1;39m([0m[39ma[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m return to[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe repo root, [0m[1;39m([0m[39mb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m copy the built fuzzer executables into `$OUT`, and [0m[1;39m([0m[39mc[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m set [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorrect execute permissions.  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Detailed Patch Steps  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. After line [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe `meson test -v` invocation[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, insert:[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      popd[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      # Ensure OSS-Fuzz output directory exists[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      mkdir -p [0m[32m"$[0m[32m{[0m[32mOUT[0m[32m}[0m[32m"[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      # Copy both fuzzers from the Meson build output into $OUT[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      cp [0m[32m"$[0m[32m{[0m[32mBUILD_DIR[0m[32m}[0m[32m/tests/libfuzzer/dav1d_fuzzer"[0m[39m \[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[32m"$[0m[32m{[0m[32mBUILD_DIR[0m[32m}[0m[32m/tests/libfuzzer/dav1d_fuzzer_mt"[0m[39m \[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[32m"$[0m[32m{[0m[32mOUT[0m[32m}[0m[32m/"[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      # Guarantee executability in the Docker container[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      chmod a+rx [0m[32m"$[0m[32m{[0m[32mOUT[0m[32m}[0m[32m/dav1d_fuzzer"[0m[39m [0m[32m"$[0m[32m{[0m[32mOUT[0m[32m}[0m[32m/dav1d_fuzzer_mt"[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. This ensures that when the Docker runner mounts `$OUT`, both binaries exist [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mat `[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer[0m[39m` and `[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer_mt[0m[39m` with the correct permissions, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39meliminating the â€œPermission deniedâ€ error.[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Justification  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By copying directly from `build/tests/libfuzzer/`, we leverage the existing [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mMeson/Ninja build artifacts without altering upstream build definitions.  [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Explicitly setting `chmod a+rx` guarantees the executables retain their [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexecute bit across Docker volume mounts.  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No fuzz harness code or third-party dependencies are touched, so existing [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtests and CI remain unaffected.  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This aligns with OSS-Fuzz expectations: `test.sh` must populate `$OUT` with [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mready-to-execute fuzzer binaries.[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects & Mitigations  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If `$OUT` is unset [0m[1;39m([0m[39munlikely in OSS-Fuzz[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, `mkdir -p [0m[32m"$[0m[32m{[0m[32mOUT[0m[32m}[0m[32m"[0m[39m` will error. [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mHowever, OSS-Fuzz always provides `$OUT`.  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The added `popd` returns the working directory to the repository root; if any [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlater lines assume being inside `build/`, those would breakâ€”but in our script there[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mare no subsequent commands.  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Should future fuzzers be added, test authors must update the copy command [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maccordingly. This can be mitigated by using a wildcard [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`dav1d_fuzzer*`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m if more [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzzers appear.[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. References  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Similar OSS-Fuzz integrations often copy binaries post-build in `test.sh`, for[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexample in many other C/C++ fuzz targets under `infra/base-images/` in the OSS-Fuzz[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrepo.  [0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No prior patches to `.aixcc/test.sh` exist, so reapplying earlier patches is [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnot required.  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The Meson build definitions [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`tests/libfuzzer/meson.build`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remain untouched, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpreserving all existing build flags and link configurations.  [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m[12/23/25 09:32:56][0m[2;36m [0m[34mINFO    [0m Prism Supervisor Routing: TeamStatus.EVALUATE -> TeamStatus.END                      ]8;id=331991;file:///home/user/crete/packages/crete/framework/agent/services/prism/__init__.py\[2m__init__.py[0m]8;;\[2m:[0m]8;id=644055;file:///home/user/crete/packages/crete/framework/agent/services/prism/__init__.py#160\[2m160[0m]8;;\
